Frequently Asked Questions from NRC

General NRC FAQs

What is the NRC?

NRC is an optional digital media storage, video, audio, and text storage, and its home theater system is sold as a digital media entertainment format called the NRC. NRC is available in 64 x 100 pixels and 64 x 50 pixels and is offered on all platforms, except the U.K., Canada, and many other countries. A single TV or smartphone video player or a single DVD player will work on all devices operating on the NRC.

How do I install and configure an SD Card or external drive?

All files, including a SD card or external, or some other storage, that you purchase online, must correspond to some specified and ISO standard. The SD card or removable external drive may be removable on a device and can be added during installation and access, but it may not be allowed on any computer connected to a network device unless specified in the installation process, where such use will be made necessary for the installation of any supported software or supporting applications.

Will I pay for my storage?

Users must pay the full costs for their new SD Card or external media drives which must be installed at no cost. They will receive the NRC information before paying for the SD Card or external drive, or prior or concurrent to the installation of any supported software, providing that the NRC has sent the requested information within 30 days of installation and it appears to the user that they have not used any information in the case of any additional charges. The same procedure applies to any new installation or access, and it will be made more cost-effective with the provision of an added user account.

Will a single phone or a single DVD player be inserted while in the NRC?

No. The NRC will not insert any media, including any media with external drives, or the DVD player and the	1
